Action VI transports typically operate in convoys or in well patrolled areas of space. Since they lack even the most basic forms of self-defensive measures, such as armour or weaponry, they are often prime targets for pirates and so rely on protection from other capital ships and starfighter escorts."

Despite its usefulness as a fleet flagship, the ship had several weaknesses, and as such, only six Inexpugnable-class ships were manufactured."
